369→def _format_halt_output(results: list[StepResult], config: RoadmapConfig) -> str:\n   370→    \"\"\"Format HALT diagnostic output per spec section 6.2.\"\"\"\n   371→    failed = [r for r in `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/commands.py`\n\n### Group structure\nThere is one Click group:\n\n- `@click.group(\"roadmap\")`\n- function: `roadmap_group()`\n\nIt currently defines only one subcommand:\n\n- `@roadmap_group.command()`\n- function: `run(...)`\n\nThere is no `validate` subcommand yet.\n\n### Group docstring\nThe group because generate is one parallel group containing 2 steps.\n\n### `run` command arguments/options\n`run(...)` takes:\n\n- positional:\n  - `spec_file: Path`\n    - `click.argument(\"spec_file\", type=click.Path(exists=True, path_type=Path))`\n\n- options:\n  - `--agents`\n    - default: `\"opus:architect,haiku:architect\"`\n    - comma-separated `model[:persona]`\n  - `--output`\n    - mapped to `output_dir`\n    - optional `Path`\n    - defaults to parent directory of spec file if omitted\n  - `--depth`\n    - choice of `quick | standard | deep`\n    - case-insensitive\n    - default `\"standard\"`\n    - used for debate depth\n  - `--resume`\n    - bool flag\n    - skips steps whose outputs already pass gates\n  - `--dry-run`\n    - bool flag\n    - prints plan and exits without subprocesses\n  - `--model`\n    - default `\"\"`\n    - described as an override model for all steps\n  - `--max-turns`\n    - int\n    - default `100`\n  - `--debug`\n    - bool flag\n    - debug with:\n  - `spec_file=spec_file.resolve()`\n  - `agents=agent_specs`\n  - `depth=depth`\n  - `output_dir=resolved_output.resolve()`\n  - `work_dir=resolved_output.resolve()`\n  - `dry_run=dry_run`\n  - `max_turns=max_turns`\n  - `model=model`\n  - `debug=debug`\n- calls `execute_roadmap(config, resume=resume)`\n\n### Important Phase 4 implication\nThere is no CLI entrypoint here for:\n- `ValidateConfig`\n- `execute_validate()`\n- validate-specific flags\n- printing validation counts/results\n\nSo CLI integration work is still outstanding.\n\n## 2) `executor.py` — `execute_roadmap()` flow and pipeline steps\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/executor.py`\n\n### Main executor flow\n`execute_roadmap(config: RoadmapConfig, resume: bool = False) -> None`\n\nFlow:\n\n1. `config.output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)`\n2. `steps = _build_steps(config)`\n3. if `config.dry_run`:\n   - `_dry_run_output(steps)`\n   - return\n4. if `resume`:\n   - imports `gate_passed` from pipeline gates\n   - `steps = _apply_resume(steps, config, gate_passed)`\n5. executes pipeline via:\n   - `execute_pipeline(...)`\n   - uses `roadmap_run_step`\n   - progress callbacks:\n     - `_print_step_start`\n     - `_print_step_complete`\n6. saves `.roadmap-state.json` via `_save_state(config, results)`\n7. if any result is `FAIL` or `TIMEOUT`:\n   - formats HALT message with `_format_halt_output(...)`\n   - prints to stderr\n   - `sys.exit(1)`\n8. otherwise prints completion summary\n\n### The 8 pipeline steps\nBuilt by `_build_steps(config)`.\n\n#### Step 1: Extract\n- id: `extract`\n- output: `extraction.md`\n- prompt: `build_extract_prompt(config.spec_file)`\n- gate: `EXTRACT_GATE`\n- timeout: 300s\n- inputs: `[config.spec_file]`\n\n#### Step 2a: Generate A\n- id: `generate-{agent_a.id}`\n- output: `roadmap-{agent_a.id}.md`\n- prompt: `build_generate_prompt(agent_a, extraction)`\n- gate: `GENERATE_A_GATE`\n- timeout: 900s\n- inputs: `[extraction]`\n- model: `agent_a.model`\n\n#### Step 2b: Generate B\n- id: `generate-{agent_b.id}`\n- output: `roadmap-{agent_b.id}.md`\n- prompt: `build_generate_prompt(agent_b, extraction)`\n- gate: `GENERATE_B_GATE`\n- timeout: 900s\n- inputs: `[extraction]`\n- model: `agent_b.model`\n\nThese two are emitted as one parallel group.\n\n#### Step 3: Diff\n- id: `diff`\n- output: `diff-analysis.md`\n- prompt: `build_diff_prompt(roadmap_a, roadmap_b)`\n- gate: `DIFF_GATE`\n- timeout: 300s\n- inputs: `[roadmap_a, roadmap_b]`\n\n#### Step 4: Debate\n- id: `debate`\n- output: `debate-transcript.md`\n- prompt: `build_debate_prompt(diff_file, roadmap_a, roadmap_b, config.depth)`\n- gate: `DEBATE_GATE`\n- timeout: 600s\n- inputs: `[diff_file, roadmap_a, roadmap_b]`\n\n#### Step 5: Score\n- id: `score`\n- output: `base-selection.md`\n- prompt: `build_score_prompt(debate_file, roadmap_a, roadmap_b)`\n- gate: `SCORE_GATE`\n- timeout: 300s\n- inputs: `[debate_file, roadmap_a, roadmap_b]`\n\n#### Step 6: Merge\n- id: `merge`\n- output: `roadmap.md`\n- prompt: `build_merge_prompt(score_file, roadmap_a, roadmap_b, debate_file)`\n- gate: `MERGE_GATE`\n- timeout: 600s\n- inputs: `[score_file, roadmap_a, roadmap_b, debate_file]`\n\n#### Step 7: Test Strategy\n- id: `test-strategy`\n- output: `test-strategy.md`\n- prompt: `build_test_strategy_prompt(merge_file, extraction)`\n- gate: `TEST_STRATEGY_GATE`\n- timeout: 300s\n- inputs: `[merge_file, extraction]`\n\n### Why the code calls it 8 steps\n`_build_steps()` returns 7 entries, but one entry is a list containing the two generate steps. So:\n- 7 pipeline entries\n- 8 individual steps\n\nTests confirm this distinction.\n\n### `roadmap_run_step(...)`\nKey behavior:\n- supports dry-run shortcut\n- embeds input file content inline when total embedded content <= 100KB\n- otherwise falls back to `--file <path>` args\n- launches `ClaudeProcess`\n- polls for cancellation\n- maps exit code:\n  - `124` -> TIMEOUT\n  - nonzero -> FAIL\n  - zero -> PASS\n- sanitizes output via `_sanitize_output()` to strip conversational preamble before frontmatter\n- injects `pipeline_diagnostics` only for the `extract` step via `_inject_pipeline_diagnostics()`\n\n## 3) `validate_executor.py` — `execute_validate()` signature and `ValidateConfig`\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/validate_executor.py`\n\n### Signature\n`execute_validate(config: ValidateConfig) -> dict`\n\nReturn shape:\n- `blocking_count: int`\n- `warning_count: int`\n- `info_count: int`\n\n### Input expectations\nIt requires these files in `config.output_dir`:\n- `roadmap.md`\n- `test-strategy.md`\n- `extraction.md`\n\nChecked by `_validate_input_files(output_dir)`.\n\nIf any are missing, it raises `FileNotFoundError`.\n\n### Output location\nValidation writes into:\n- `<output_dir>/validate/`\n\nPrimary output report:\n- `<output_dir>/validate/validation-report.md`\n\n### Routing behavior\n`execute_validate()` branches by `len(config.agents)`:\n\n#### Single-agent mode\nUses `_build_single_agent_steps(...)`:\n- one step only:\n  - id: `reflect`\n  - output: `validate/validation-report.md`\n  - gate: `REFLECT_GATE`\n  - timeout: 600s\n  - inputs: `[roadmap.md, test-strategy.md, extraction.md]`\n  - model: `config.agents[0].model`\n\n#### Multi-agent mode\nUses `_build_multi_agent_steps(...)`:\n- first entry: parallel reflection steps, one per agent\n  - ids: `reflect-{agent.id}`\n  - outputs: `validate/reflect-{agent.id}.md`\n  - gate: `REFLECT_GATE`\n  - timeout: 600s\n  - inputs: all 3 pipeline files\n  - model: agent-specific\n- second entry: sequential merge step\n  - id: `adversarial-merge`\n  - output: `validate/validation-report.md`\n  - gate: `ADVERSARIAL_MERGE_GATE`\n  - timeout: 600s\n  - inputs: reflection output files\n  - prompt built from reflection report paths\n\n### Step runner\n`validate_run_step(...)` mirrors `roadmap_run_step(...)`:\n- dry-run shortcut\n- inline embedding up to 100KB\n- falls back to `--file`\n- launches `ClaudeProcess`\n- sanitizes output after success\n- does not inject any extra frontmatter like roadmap extract does\n\n### Partial failure behavior\nIf failures occur in multi-agent mode:\n- `execute_validate()` writes a degraded report via `_write_degraded_report(...)`\n- report is explicitly marked:\n  - `validation_complete: false`\n- includes:\n  - failed agent ids\n  - passed agent ids\n  - warning banner\n- returns parsed counts from that degraded report\n\nIf failures occur in single-agent mode:\n- it logs the failure\n- still returns parsed counts from report path, which may be zeros if report missing/unparseable\n\n### Count parsing\n`_parse_report_counts(report_path)`:\n- reads frontmatter\n- parses:\n  - `blocking_issues_count`\n  - `warnings_count`\n- counts INFO findings by scanning body for `[INFO]`\n\n## 4) `validate_gates.py` — gate structures\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/validate_gates.py`\n\nThere are two gates.\n\n### `REFLECT_GATE`\n- type: `GateCriteria`\n- required frontmatter:\n  - `blocking_issues_count`\n  - `warnings_count`\n  - `tasklist_ready`\n- `min_lines=20`\n- `enforcement_tier=\"STANDARD\"`\n- semantic checks:\n  - `frontmatter_values_non_empty`\n    - reuses `_frontmatter_values_non_empty` from roadmap gates\n\n### `ADVERSARIAL_MERGE_GATE`\n- type: `GateCriteria`\n- required frontmatter:\n  - `blocking_issues_count`\n  - `warnings_count`\n  - `tasklist_ready`\n  - `validation_mode`\n  - `validation_agents`\n- `min_lines=30`\n- `enforcement_tier=\"STRICT\"`\n- semantic checks:\n  - `frontmatter_values_non_empty`\n  - `agreement_table_present`\n\n### Agreement table semantic\nHelper:\n- `_has_agreement_table(content: str) -> bool`\n\nIt looks for:\n- a pipe-delimited line containing `agree` or `agreement`\n- followed by a separator row containing `|` and `-`\n\nSo it is a lightweight markdown-table presence check, not a deep schema validator.\n\n## 5) `validate_prompts.py` — prompt structures\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/validate_prompts.py`\n\nThere are two pure prompt builders.\n\n### `build_reflect_prompt(roadmap: str, test_strategy: str, extraction: str) -> str`\nStructure:\n\n- persona framing:\n  - “You are a validation specialist. You did NOT generate these artifacts.”\n- instructs the model to read roadmap, test-strategy, extraction\n- asks validation across 7 dimensions\n\n#### 5 BLOCKING dimensions\n1. Schema\n2. Structure\n3. Traceability\n4. Cross-file consistency\n5. Parseability\n\n#### 2 WARNING dimensions\n6. Interleave\n   - explicitly defines formula:\n     - `interleave_ratio = unique_phases_with_deliverables / total_phases`\n   - must be in `[0.1, 1.0]`\n   - warns against back-loaded test activities\n7. Decomposition\n   - flags compound deliverables, especially joined by “and” / “or”\n\n#### Required output format\nYAML frontmatter:\n- `blocking_issues_count`\n- `warnings_count`\n- `tasklist_ready`\n\nThen sections:\n- `## Findings`\n- `## Summary`\n- `## Interleave Ratio`\n\nEach finding requires:\n- severity\n- dimension name\n- description\n- location\n- evidence\n- fix guidance\n\n### `build_merge_prompt(reflect_reports: list[str]) -> str`\nStructure:\n\n- persona framing:\n  - “adversarial merge specialist”\n- merge categories:\n  - `BOTH_AGREE`\n  - `ONLY_A`\n  - `ONLY_B`\n  - `CONFLICT`\n- explicitly asks for an agreement table\n\n#### Required frontmatter\n- `blocking_issues_count`\n- `warnings_count`\n- `tasklist_ready`\n- `validation_mode: adversarial`\n- `validation_agents: ...`\n\n#### Required sections\n- `## Agreement Table`\n- `## Consolidated Findings`\n- `## Summary`\n\n### Important Phase 4 implication\nThese prompts are ready for executor use, but there is no CLI-facing command yet that constructs validation config and invokes this flow.\n\n## 6) `models.py` — data models including `ValidateConfig`\n\nFile:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/roadmap/models.py`\n\n### `AgentSpec`\nFields:\n- `model: str`\n- `persona: str`\n\nMethods/properties:\n- `AgentSpec.parse(spec: str) -> AgentSpec`\n  - `\"model:persona\"` -> split both\n  - `\"model\"` -> defaults `persona=\"architect\"`\n- `id` property\n  - returns `\"model-persona\"`\n\nExamples:\n- `opus:architect` -> `AgentSpec(\"opus\", \"architect\")`\n- `haiku` -> `AgentSpec(\"haiku\", \"architect\")`\n\n### `RoadmapConfig`\nDataclass extending `PipelineConfig`\n\nAdds:\n- `spec_file: Path`\n- `agents: list[AgentSpec]`\n  - `build_test_strategy_prompt(merge_file, extraction)`\n- gate: `TEST_STRATEGY_GATE`\n- timeout: 300s\n- inputs: `[merge_file, extraction]`\n\n### Why the code calls it 8 steps\n`_build_steps()` returns 7 entries, but one entry is a list containing the two generate steps. So:\n- 7 pipeline entries\n- 8 individual steps\n\nTests confirm this distinction.\n\n### `roadmap_run_step(...)`\nKey behavior:\n- supports dry-run shortcut\n- embeds input file content inline when total embedded content <= 100KB\n- otherwise falls back to `--file <path>` args\n- launches `ClaudeProcess`\n- polls for cancellation\n- maps exit code:\n  -  if content.lstrip().startswith(\"---\"):\n    89→        return 0\n    90→\n    91→    # Search for the first ^--- line\n    92→    match = re.search(r\"^---[ \\t]*$\", content, re.MULTILINE)\n    93→    if match is None:\n    94→        # No frontmatter found at all -- leave file unchanged\n    95→        return 0\n    96→\n    97→    preamble = content[: match.start()]\n    98→    cleaned = content[match.start() :]\n    99→    preamble_bytes = len(preamble.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n   100→\n   101→    # Atomic write: tmp file + os.replace\n   102→    tmp_file = _log.info(\"Stripped %d-byte preamble from %s\", preamble_bytes, output_file)\n   107→    return preamble_bytes\n   108→\n   109→\n   110→def _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(\n   111→    output_file: Path,\n   112→    started_at: datetime,\n   113→    finished_at: datetime,\n   114→) -> None:\n   115→    \"\"\"Inject executor-populated pipeline_diagnostics into extraction frontmatter.\n   116→\n   117→    The LLM cannot reliably produce execution timing or environment metadata,\n   118→    so the executor injects these fields post-subprocess (FR-033).\n   119→    \"\"\"\n   120→    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   121→    if not content.startswith(\"---\"):\n   122→        return\n   123→\n   124→    # Find end of frontmatter\n   125→    end_idx = content.find(\"\\n---\", 3)\n   126→    if end_idx == -1:\n   127→        return\n   128→\n   129→    elapsed = (finished_at - started_at).total_seconds()\n   130→    diagnostics_line = (\n   131→        f\"pipeline_diagnostics: \"\n   132→        f\"{{elapsed_seconds: {elapsed:.1f}, \"\n   133→        f\"started_at: \\\"{started_at.isoformat()}\\\", \"\n   134→        f\"finished_at: \\\"{finished_at.isoformat()}\\\"}}\"\n   135→    )\n   136→\n   137→    # Insert before the closing ---\n   138→    new_content = (\n   139→        content[: end_idx]\n   140→        + \"\\n\"\n   141→        + diagnostics_line\n   142→        + content[end_idx:]\n   143→    )\n   144→    output_file.write_text(new_content, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   145→\n   146→\n   147→def roadmap_run_step(\n   148→    step: Step,\n   149→    config: PipelineConfig,\n   150→    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n   151→) -> StepResult:\n   152→    \"\"\"Execute a single roadmap step as a Claude subprocess.\n   153→\n   154→    Builds argv with context isolation, launches process, waits with\n   155→    timeout, and returns StepResult.\n   156→    \"\"\"\n   157→    started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   158→\n   159→    if config.dry_run:\n   160→        _log.info(\"[dry-run] Would execute step '%s'\", step.id)\n   161→        return StepResult(\n   162→            step=step,\n   163→            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   164→            attempt=1,\n   165→            started_at=started_at,\n   166→            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   167→        )\n   168→\n   169→    # Inline embedding: read input files into the prompt instead of --file flags\n   170→    embedded = _embed_inputs(step.inputs)\n   171→    if embedded and len(embedded.encode(\"utf-8\")) <= _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT:\n   172→        effective_prompt = step.prompt + \"\\n\\n\" + embedded\n   173→        extra_args: list[str] = []\n   174→    elif embedded:\n   175→        _log.warning(\n   176→            \"Step '%s': embedded inputs exceed %d bytes, falling back to --file flags\",\n   177→            step.id,\n   178→            _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT,\n   179→        )\n   180→        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n   181→        extra_args = [\n   182→            arg\n   183→            for input_path in step.inputs\n   184→            for arg in (\"--file\", str(input_path))\n   185→        ]\n   186→    else:\n   187→        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n   188→        extra_args = []\n   189→\n   190→    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n   191→        prompt=effective_prompt,\n   192→        output_file=step.output_file,\n   193→        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n   194→        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n   195→        model=step.model or config.model,\n   196→        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n   197→        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n   198→        output_format=\"text\",\n   199→        extra_args=extra_args,\n   200→    )\n   201→\n   202→    proc.start()\n   203→\n   204→    # Poll for cancellation while waiting\n   205→    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n   206→        if cancel_check():\n   207→            proc.terminate()\n   208→            return StepResult(\n   209→                step=step,\n   210→                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n   211→                attempt=1,\n   212→                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n   213→                started_at=started_at,\n   214→                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   215→            )\n   216→        time.sleep(1)\n   217→\n   218→    exit_code = proc.wait()\n   219→    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   220→\n   221→    if exit_code == 124:\n   222→        return StepResult(\n   223→            step=step,\n   224→            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n   225→ finished_at=finished_at,\n   229→        )\n   230→\n   231→    if exit_code != 0:\n   232→        return StepResult(\n   233→            step=step,\n   234→            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n   235→            attempt=1,\n   236→            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' exited with code {exit_code}\",\n   237→            started_at=started_at,\n   238→            finished_at=finished_at,\n   239→        )\n   240→\n   241→    # Sanitize output: strip conversational preamble before gate validation\n   242→    _sanitize_output(step.output_file)\n   243→\n   244→    # Inject executor-populated fields into extract step frontmatter (FR-033)\n   245→    if step.id == \"extract\" and step.output_file.exists():\n   246→        _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(step.output_file, started_at, finished_at)\n   247→\n   248→    # Process completed successfully; gate check happens in execute_pipeline\n   249→    return StepResult(\n   250→        step=step,\n   251→        status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   252→        attempt=1,\n   253→        started_at=started_at,\n   254→        finished_at=finished_at,\n   255→    )\n   256→\n 369→def _format_halt_output(results: list[StepResult], config: RoadmapConfig) -> str:\n   370→    \"\"\"Format HALT diagnostic output per spec section 6.2.\"\"\"\n   371→    failed = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n   372→    passed = [r for r in results if r.status == StepStatus.PASS]\n   373→    cancelled = [r for r in results if r.status == StepStatus.CANCELLED]\n   374→\n   375→    if not failed:\n   376→        return \"\"\n   377→\n   378→    fail = failed[-1]\n   379→    step = fail.step\n   380→\n   381→    # Calculate file details len(content.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n   386→        line_count = len(content.splitlines())\n   387→        file_info = f\"  Output size: {byte_count} bytes ({line_count} lines)\\n\"\n   388→    elif step:\n   389→        file_info = \"  Output file: not created\\n\"\n   390→\n   391→    elapsed = f\"{fail.duration_seconds:.0f}s\"\n   392→\n   393→    lines = [\n   394→        f\"ERROR: Roadmap pipeline halted at step '{step.id}' (attempt {fail.attempt}/2)\",\n   395→        f\"  Gate failure: {fail.gate_failure_reason}\",\n   396→        f\"  Output file: {step.output_file}\",\n   397→        file_info.rstrip(),\n   398→        f\"  Step timeout: {step.timeout_seconds}s | Elapsed: {elapsed}\",\n   399→        \"\",\n   400→        f\"Completed steps: {', '.join(f'{r.step.id} (PASS, attempt {r.attempt})' for r in passed) or 'none'}\",\n   401→        f\"Failed step:     {step.id} ({fail.status.value}, attempt {fail.attempt})\",\n   402→    ]\n   403→\n   404→    # Collect skipped steps\n   405→    all_step_ids = _get_all_step_ids(config)\n   406→    executed_ids = {r.step.id for r in results}\n   407→    skipped_ids = [sid for sid in all_step_ids if sid not in executed_ids]\n --resume\",\n   418→        \"\",\n   419→        \"To inspect the failing output:\",\n   420→        f\"  cat {step.output_file}\",\n   421→    ])\n   422→\n   423→    return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n = config.agents[1] if len(config.agents) > 1 else config.agents[0]\n   430→    return [\n   431→        \"extract\",\n   432→        f\"generate-{agent_a.id}\",\n   433→        f\"generate-{agent_b.id}\",\n   434→        \"diff\",\n   435→        \"debate\",\n   436→        \"score\",\n   437→        \"merge\",\n   438→        \"test-strategy\",\n   439→    ]\n   440→\n   441→\n   442→def _print_step_start(step: Step) -> None:\n   443→    \"\"\"Print progress output when a step starts.\"\"\"\n   444→    print(f\"[roadmap] Starting step: {step.id}\", flush=True)\n   445→\n   446→\n   447→def _print_step_complete(step: Step, result: StepResult) -> None:\n   448→    \"\"\"Print progress output when a step completes.\"\"\"\n   449→    duration = {result.gate_failure_reason}\", flush=True)\n   462→\n   463→\n   464→def _dry_run_output(steps: list[Step | list[Step]]) -> None:\n   465→    \"\"\"Print step plan and gate criteria for 494→\n   495→\n   496→def _save_state(config: RoadmapConfig, results: list[StepResult]) -> None:\n   497→    \"\"\"Write .roadmap-state.json to output_dir via atomic tmp + os.replace().\"\"\"\n   498→ },\n   519→    }\n   520→\n   521→    write_state(state, state_file)\n   522→\n   523→\n   524→def write_state(state: dict, path: Path) -> None:\n   525→    \"\"\"Write state dict to path atomically via tmp file + os.replace().\"\"\"\n   526→    import os as _os\n   527→\n   528→    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n   529→    tmp = path.with_suffix(\".tmp\")\n   530→    tmp.write_text(json.dumps(state, indent=2), encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   531→    _os.replace(str(tmp), str(path))\n   532→\n   533→\n   534→def read_state(path: Path) -> dict | None:\n   535→    \"\"\"Read state from path with graceful recovery on missing/malformed files.\"\"\"\n   536→    if not path.exists():\n   537→        return None\n   538→    try:\n   539→        text = path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   540→        if not text.strip():\n   541→            return None\n   542→        return json.loads(text)\n   543→    except (json.JSONDecodeError, OSError):\n   544→        return None\n   545→\n   546→\n   547→def apply_decomposition_pass(deliverables: list[Deliverable]) -> list[Deliverable]:\n   548→    \"\"\"Post-generation decomposition pass for the roadmap pipeline.\n   549→\n   550→    Runs after deliverable generation, before output formatting.\n   551→    Splits behavioral deliverables into Implement/Verify pairs.\n   552→\n   553→    Idempotent: running twice produces identical results because\n   554→    already-decomposed deliverables (IDs ending .a/.b) are skipped.\n   555→\n   556→    Preserves milestone-internal ordering: deliverables within each\n   557→    milestone maintain their relative order after decomposition.\n   558→    \"\"\"\n   559→    return decompose_deliverables(deliverables)\n   560→\n   561→\n   562→def execute_roadmap(config: RoadmapConfig, resume: bool = False) -> None:\n   563→    \"\"\"Execute the roadmap generation pipeline.\n   564→\n   565→    Builds the step list, handles --dry-run and --resume, then\n   566→    delegates to execute_pipeline() with roadmap_run_step.\n   567→    \"\"\"\n   568→    config.output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n   569→\n   570→    steps = _build_steps(config)\n   571→\n   572→    # --dry-run: print plan and exit\n   573→    if config.dry_run:\n   574→        _dry_run_output(steps)\n   575→        return\n   576→\n   577→    # --resume: check which steps already pass their gates\n   578→    if resume:\n   579→        from ..pipeline.gates import gate_passed\n   580→\n   581→        steps = _apply_resume(steps, config, gate_passed)\n   582→\n   583→    # Execute pipeline\n   584→    results = execute_pipeline(\n   585→        steps=steps,\n   586→        config=config,\n   587→        run_step=roadmap_run_step,\n   588→        on_step_start=_print_step_start,\n   589→        on_step_complete=_print_step_complete,\n   590→    )\n   591→\n   592→    # Save state\n   593→    _save_state(config, results)\n   594→\n   595→    # Check for failures\n   596→    failures = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n   597→    if failures:\n   598→        halt_msg = _format_halt_output(results, config)\n   599→        print(halt_msg, file=sys.stderr)\n   600→        sys.exit(1)\n   601→\n   602→    print(f\"\\n[roadmap] Pipeline complete: {len(results)} steps passed\", flush=True)\n   603→\n   604→\n   605→def _apply_resume(\n   606→    steps: list[Step | list[Step]],\n   607→    config: RoadmapConfig,\n   608→    gate_fn: Callable,\n   609→) -> list[Step | list[Step]]:\n   610→    \"\"\"Apply --resume logic: skip steps whose outputs already pass gates.\n   611→\n   612→    Also checks for stale spec detection.\n   613→    \"\"\"\n   614→    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n   615→    state = read_state(state_file)\n   616→    force_extract = False\n   617→    if state is not None:\n   618→        saved_hash = state.get(\"spec_hash\", \"\")\n   619→        current_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n   620→        if saved_hash and saved_hash != current_hash:\n   621→            print(\n   622→                f\"WARNING: spec-file has changed since last run.\\n\"\n   623→                f\"  Last hash: {saved_hash[:12]}...\\n\"\n   624→                f\"  Current:   {current_hash[:12]}...\\n\"\n   625→                f\"Forcing re-run of extract step.\",\n   626→                file=sys.stderr,\n   627→                flush=True,\n   628→            )\n   629→            force_extract = True\n   630→\n   631→    skipped = 0\n   632→    result: list[Step | list[Step]] = []\n   633→    found_failure = False\n   634→\n   635→    for entry in steps:\n   636→        if found_failure:\n   637→            # After first failing step, include all remaining steps\n   638→            result.append(entry)\n   639→            continue\n   640→\n   641→        if isinstance(entry, list):\n   642→            # Parallel group: check all steps\n   643→            all_pass = True\n   644→            for s in entry:\n   645→                if s.gate:\n   646→                    passed, _reason = gate_fn(s.output_file, s.gate)\n   647→                    if not passed:\n   648→                        all_pass = False\n   649→                        break\n   650→                else:\n   651→                    all_pass = False\n   652→                    break\n   653→            if all_pass:\n   654→                skipped += len(entry)\n   655→                print(f\"[roadmap] Skipping {', '.join(s.id for s in entry)} (gates pass)\", flush=True)\n   656→            else:\n   657→                found_failure = True\n   658→                result.append(entry)\n   659→        else:\n   660→            # Force re-run of extract on stale spec\n   661→            if force_extract and entry.id == \"extract\":\n   662→                found_failure = True\n   663→                result.append(entry)\n   664→                continue\n   665→\n   666→            if entry.gate:\n   667→                passed, _reason = gate_fn(entry.output_file, entry.gate)\n   668→                if passed:\n   669→                    skipped += 1\n   670→                    print(f\"[roadmap] Skipping {entry.id} (gate passes)\", flush=True)\n   671→                    continue\n   672→ Uses atomic write (write to ``.tmp`` then ``os.replace()``) to prevent\n    partial file states.\n\n    Returns the byte count of the stripped preamble (0 when file already starts\n    with ``---`` or roadmap_run_step(\n    step: Step,\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n) -> StepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute a single roadmap step as a Claude subprocess.\n\n    Builds argv with context isolation, launches process, waits with\n    timeout, and returns StepResult.\n    \"\"\"\n    started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if config.dry_run:\n        _log.info(\"[dry-run] Would execute step '%s'\", step.id)\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n            attempt=1,\n )\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = [\n            arg\n            for input_path in step.inputs\n            for arg in (\"--file\", str(input_path))\n        ]\n    else:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = []\n\n    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n        prompt=effective_prompt,\n        output_file=step.output_file,\n        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=step.model or config.model,\n        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n        output_format=\"text\",\n        extra_args=extra_args,\n    )\n\n    proc.start()\n\n    # Poll for cancellation while waiting\n    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n        if cancel_check():\n            proc.terminate()\n            return StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n                attempt=1,\n                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n            )\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n    exit_code = proc.wait()\n    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' timed out after {step.timeout_seconds}s\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' exited with code {exit_code}\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    # 100 KB\n\n\ndef _embed_inputs(input_paths: list[Path]) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Read input files and return their contents as fenced code blocks.\n\n    Each file is wrapped in a fenced block with a ``# <path>`` header.\n    Returns an empty string when *input_paths* is empty (no-op).\n    \"\"\"\n    if not input_paths:\n        return \"\"\n\n    blocks: list[str] = []\n    for p in input_paths:\n        content = Path(p).read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n        blocks.append(f\"# {p}\\n```\\n{content}\\n```\")\n    return \"\\n\\n\".join(blocks)\n\n\ndef _sanitize_output(output_file: Path) -> int:\n    \"\"\"Strip conversational preamble before YAML frontmatter in a step output file.\n\n    Reads the file, finds the first ``^---`` line, and removes everything before\n    it.  Uses atomic write (write to ``.tmp`` then ``os.replace()``) to prevent\n    partial file states.\n\n    Returns the byte count of the stripped preamble (0 when file already starts\n    with ``---`` or no frontmatter delimiter is found).\n    \"\"\"\n    import os\n    import re\n\n    try:\n        content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    except FileNotFoundError:\n        return 0\n\n    # Already starts with frontmatter delimiter -- nothing to strip\n    if content.lstrip().startswith(\"---\"):\n        return 0\n\n    # Search for the first ^--- line\n    match = re.search(r\"^---[ \\t]*$\", content, re.MULTILINE)\n    if match is None:\n        # No frontmatter found at all -- leave file unchanged\n        return 0\n\n    preamble = content[: match.start()]\n    cleaned = content[match.start() :]\n    preamble_bytes = len(preamble.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n\n    # Atomic write: tmp file + os.replace\n    tmp_file = output_file.with_suffix(output_file.suffix + \".tmp\")\n    tmp_file.write_text(cleaned, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    os.replace(tmp_file, output_file)\n\n    _log.info(\"Stripped %d-byte preamble from %s\", preamble_bytes, output_file)\n    return preamble_bytes\n\n\ndef _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(\n    output_file: Path,\n    started_at: datetime,\n    finished_at: datetime,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Inject executor-populated pipeline_diagnostics into extraction frontmatter.\n\n    The LLM cannot reliably produce execution timing or environment metadata,\n    so the executor injects these fields post-subprocess (FR-033).\n    \"\"\"\n    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    if not content.startswith(\"---\"):\n        return\n\n    # Find end of frontmatter\n    end_idx = content.find(\"\\n---\", 3)\n    if end_idx == -1:\n        return\n\n    elapsed = (finished_at - started_at).total_seconds()\n    diagnostics_line = (\n        f\"pipeline_diagnostics: \"\n        f\"{{elapsed_seconds: roadmap_run_step(\n    step: Step,\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n) -> StepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute a single roadmap step as a Claude subprocess.\n\n    Builds argv with context isolation, launches process, waits with\n    timeout, and returns StepResult.\n    \"\"\"\n    started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if config.dry_run:\n        _log.info(\"[dry-run] Would execute step '%s'\", step.id)\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n            attempt=1,\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n        )\n\n    # Inline embedding: read input files into the prompt instead of --file flags\n    embedded = _embed_inputs(step.inputs)\n    if embedded and len(embedded.encode(\"utf-8\")) <= _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt + \"\\n\\n\" + embedded\n        extra_args: list[str] = []\n    elif embedded:\n        _log.warning(\n            \"Step '%s': embedded inputs exceed %d bytes, falling back to --file flags\",\n            step.id,\n            _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT,\n        )\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = [\n            arg\n            for input_path in step.inputs\n            for arg in (\"--file\", str(input_path))\n        ]\n    else:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = []\n\n    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n        prompt=effective_prompt,\n        output_file=step.output_file,\n        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=step.model or config.model,\n        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n        output_format=\"text\",\n        extra_args=extra_args,\n    )\n\n    proc.start()\n\n    # Poll for cancellation while waiting\n    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n        if cancel_check():\n            proc.terminate()\n            return StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n                attempt=1,\n                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n            )\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n    exit_code = proc.wait()\n    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' timed out after {step.timeout_seconds}s\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' exited with code {exit_code}\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    # execute_pipeline\n    return StepResult(\n        step=step,\n        status=StepStatus.PASS,\n        attempt=1,\n        started_at=started_at,\n        finished_at=finished_at,\n    )\n\n\ndef (sequential)\n    or a list[Step] (parallel group).\n    \"\"\"\n    out = config.output_dir\n\n    # Agent specs\n    agent_a = config.agents[0]\n    agent_b = config.agents[1] if len(config.agents) \"\"\"Strip conversational preamble before YAML frontmatter in a step output file.\n\n    Reads the file, finds the first ``^---`` line, and removes everything before\n    it.  Uses atomic write (write to ``.tmp`` then ``os.replace()``) to prevent\n    partial file states.\n\n    Returns the byte count of the stripped preamble (0 when file already starts\n    with ``---`` or no frontmatter delimiter is found).\n    \"\"\"\n    import os\n    import re\n\n    try:\n        content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    except FileNotFoundError:\n        return roadmap_run_step(\n    step: Step,\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n) -> StepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute a single roadmap step as a Claude subprocess.\n\n    Builds argv with context isolation, launches process, waits with\n    timeout, and returns StepResult.\n    \"\"\"\n    started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if config.dry_run:\n        _log.info(\"[dry-run] Would execute step '%s'\", step.id)\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n            attempt=1,\n )\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = [\n            arg\n            for input_path in step.inputs\n            for arg in (\"--file\", str(input_path))\n        ]\n    else:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = []\n\n    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n        prompt=effective_prompt,\n        output_file=step.output_file,\n        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=step.model or config.model,\n        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n        output_format=\"text\",\n        extra_args=extra_args,\n    )\n\n    proc.start()\n\n    # Poll for cancellation while waiting\n    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n        if cancel_check():\n            proc.terminate()\n            return StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n                attempt=1,\n                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n            )\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n    exit_code = proc.wait()\n    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' timed out after {step.timeout_seconds}s\",\n Step, result: StepResult) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Print progress output when a step completes.\"\"\"\n    duration = f\"{result.duration_seconds:.0f}s\"\n    if result.status == StepStatus.PASS:\n for entry in steps:\n        if isinstance(entry, list):\n            for s in entry:\n                step_num += 1\n                _print_step_plan(step_num, s, parallel=True)\n        else:\n            step_num += 1\n            _print_step_plan(step_num, entry)\n\n\ndef _print_step_plan(num: int, step: Step, parallel: bool = False) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Print a single step's plan entry.\"\"\"\n
